<script>
$("#menu-toggle, .ega-overlay").click(function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
let $menu = $('#ega-menu--mb, .ega-overlay');
$menu.toggleClass("ega-show");
});

$('#ega-menu--mb ul a span').click(function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
$(this).parent().next().toggle(200);
if($(this).text() == '+') {
$(this).text('-');
} else {
$(this).text('+');
}
});
</script>

EGA.preloader = () => {


}
EGA.start = () => {
EGA.preloader();
EGA.scrolltotop();
EGA.modal.open();
EGA.modal.close();
EGA.tabs.init();
EGA.dropdown.open();
EGA.switchForm();
EGA.alertSubmit();
}
window.addEventListener('load', function() {

$(window).on('scroll', function() {
EGA.sticky({ $header_el : ".ega-header", element_offset : 40 });
})
})

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
EGA.start();

/*var paramHeader = {
'url': '/?view=indexView',
'type': 'GET',
'success': function (data) {
$('head').eq(0).append(data)

}
};*/

var paramSubscribe = {
'url': '/?view=subscribe',
'type': 'GET',
'success': function (data) {
data = data.replace( /<script(.*?)>(.*?)<\/script>/gi, function(string){
if(string.includes('grecaptcha.ready')){
let recaptchaScript = $(string).text()
recaptchaScript = `<script>setTimeout(function(){${recaptchaScript}},5000)<\/script>`
return recaptchaScript
}
return string
})
$('#ega_form_cusomer').html(data)
}
}

setTimeout(function () {
$.ajax(paramSubscribe)
}, 5000)



$('#modal-campaign .ega-modal__close').click(function(){
sessionStorage.setItem('popup_campaign', 'seen');
})

$('#menu-toggle').click(function(){
$('#ega-fashion').toggleClass("menu-is-opened");
})
$('.blog_review__item').click(function(e){
e.preventDefault();

var urlHanlde = $(this).find("a").data().handle;

$.ajax({
url: urlHanlde + "?view=review",
success: function(review_template){
var author="",
content="",
date="",
pdImg="",
pdTitle="",
pdUrl="";

$(review_template).find("tbody tr").map(function(i,v){
$(v).find("td").map(function(k,val){
if(i==0){
author = $(v).find("td").eq(0).text();
content = $(v).find("td").eq(1).text();
date = $(v).find("td").eq(2).text();
}

if(i==1){
pdImg = $(v).find("td").eq(0).find("img").attr("src");
pdTitle = $(v).find("td").eq(1).text();
pdUrl = $(v).find("td").eq(2).text();
}
})
})

var artImg = $(review_template).find("#artice-img").attr("src");

$('.review__img img').attr("src",artImg);

$('.review__body h3').text(author);
$('.review__body .review-text').text(content);
$('.review__body .review-date').text(date);
pdImg && pdImg.trim() ? $('.review__product .review-pd-img img').attr("src",pdImg).show() : $('.review__product .review-pd-img img').attr("src",pdImg).hide();
$('.review__product .review-pd-info h3').text(pdTitle);
$('.review__product .review-pd-info a').attr("href",pdUrl);

EGA.modal.openModalById('blog-review-popup');

}
})
})
$('.over').click(function(){
$('#ega-fashion').removeClass("menu-is-opened");
$('body').removeClass('filter-mb-opened');
})


var body = $('body');
var topbar = $('#topbar');

}, 500);
})

body.toggleClass('show-search');
})


})

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
$(".js-collapse-footer").click(function( event ) {
event.preventDefault();
$(this).toggleClass('toogled')
if($(this).hasClass('toogled')){
$(this).find('span').html(`<svg class="ega-ic-angle-up"><use xlink:href="#ega-ic-angle-up"></use></svg>`)
}else{
$(this).find('span').html(`<svg class="ega-ic-angle-down"><use xlink:href="#ega-ic-angle-down"></use></svg>`)
}
var ul = $(this).next('ul');
ul.toggle(300);
});
function horizontalNav () {
return {
wrapper: $('.navigation--horizontal .navigation-wrapper'),
navigation: $('.navigation--horizontal .navigation'),
item: $('.navigation--horizontal .navigation .ega-menu__item'),
arrows: $('.navigation-arrows'),
scrollStep: 0,
totalStep: 0,
transform: function(){
return `translateY(-${this.scrollStep*100}%)`
},
onCalcNavOverView: function(){
let itemHeight = this.item.eq(0).outerHeight(),
navHeight = this.navigation.height()
return Math.ceil(navHeight/itemHeight)
},
handleArrowClick: function(e){
this.totalStep = this.onCalcNavOverView()
this.scrollStep = $(e.target).parents(".ega-nav-scroll").hasClass("prev") ? this.scrollStep - 1 : this.scrollStep + 1
this.handleScroll()
},
handleScroll: function(){
this.arrows.find('.ega-nav-scroll').removeClass('disabled')
if(this.totalStep - 1 <= this.scrollStep ){
this.arrows.find('.next').addClass('disabled')
this.scrollStep = this.totalStep - 1
}
if(this.scrollStep <= 0){
this.arrows.find('.prev').addClass('disabled')
this.scrollStep = 0
}
this.item.find('.ega-menu__link:not(.sub-menu)').css('transform', this.transform())
},
init:function(){
this.totalStep = this.onCalcNavOverView()
if(this.totalStep > 1){
this.wrapper.addClass('overflow')
}
this.handleScroll()
this.arrows.find('.ega-nav-scroll').click((e)=>this.handleArrowClick(e))
}
}
}
//check menu
if(window.matchMedia('(min-width: 992px)').matches){
horizontalNav().init()
$(window).on('resize',()=>horizontalNav().init())
}
})
</script>
